~/STAR-2.7.0f/bin/Linux_x86_64/STAR --genomeDir /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/ --readFilesIn sortmerna/sort_UNC-CR-R9-d9_1.fastq --runThreadN 10 --outFileNamePrefix STAR/UNC-CR-R9-d9/UNC-CR-R9-d9 --outFilterMultimapNmax 1 --outSAMtype BAM SortedByCoordinate;
pigz -p 12 sortmerna/sort_UNC-CR-R9-d9_1.fastq;
cp STAR/UNC-CR-R9-d9/UNC-CR-R9-d9Log.final.out log/UNC-CR-R9-d9_STAR.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes STAR/UNC-CR-R9-d9/UNC-CR-R9-d9Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count/UNC-CR-R9-d9_union_name.count;
~/fastq_screen_v0.11.1/fastq_screen --aligner bwa --threads 10 --conf /mnt/f/Genomes/fastq_screen/fastq_screen.conf sortmerna/sort_UNC-CR-R9-d9_1.fastq.gz;
mv sort_UNC-CR-R9-d9_1_screen* qa/fastq_screen;
samtools index STAR/UNC-CR-R9-d9/UNC-CR-R9-d9Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam;
umi_tools dedup -I STAR/UNC-CR-R9-d9/UNC-CR-R9-d9Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam --output-stats=log/dedup/UNC-CR-R9-d9 -S umitools/UNC-CR-R9-d9-deduplicated.bam > log/UNC-CR-R9-d9_dedup.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes umitools/UNC-CR-R9-d9-deduplicated.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count_umi/UNC-CR-R9-d9_union_name.count;
umi_tools extract --stdin=raw/UNC-R15-d3_1.fastq.gz --bc-pattern="^(?P<umi_1>.{6})(?P<discard_1>TATA){e<=1}" --extract-method=regex --log=log/UNC-R15-d3_umi-tools.log --stdout umitools/umi_UNC-R15-d3_1.fastq.gz;
fastqc -o qa/umitools umitools/umi_UNC-R15-d3_1.fastq.gz;
TrimmomaticSE -threads 10 -phred33 umitools/umi_UNC-R15-d3_1.fastq.gz trimmomatic/TRIM_UNC-R15-d3_1.fastq HEADCROP:12 ILLUMINACLIP:/mnt/d/Adapters/Lexogen_quantseq.fa:2:30:10 LEADING:3 TRAILING:3 SLIDINGWINDOW:4:15 MINLEN:36 2> log/UNC-R15-d3_trim.log;
fastqc -o qa/trimmomatic trimmomatic/TRIM_UNC-R15-d3_1.fastq;
time sortmerna --ref /mnt/d/rRNA_database/mtDNA_homo_sapiens.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/mtDNA_homo_sapiens:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5.8s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5.8s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-16s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-16s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-16s-id90.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-16s-id90:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-18s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-18s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-28s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-28s-id98 --reads trimmomatic/TRIM_UNC-R15-d3_1.fastq --aligned UNC-R15-d3_aligned --other UNC-R15-d3_sortmerna --log -a 10 -v --fastx;
mv UNC-R15-d3_sortmerna.fastq sortmerna/sort_UNC-R15-d3_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 trimmomatic/TRIM_UNC-R15-d3_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 UNC-R15-d3_aligned.fastq;

cp STAR/UNC-CR-R15-d3/UNC-CR-R15-d3Log.final.out log/UNC-CR-R15-d3_STAR.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes STAR/UNC-CR-R15-d3/UNC-CR-R15-d3Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count/UNC-CR-R15-d3_union_name.count;
~/fastq_screen_v0.11.1/fastq_screen --aligner bwa --threads 10 --conf /mnt/f/Genomes/fastq_screen/fastq_screen.conf sortmerna/sort_UNC-CR-R15-d3_1.fastq.gz;
mv sort_UNC-CR-R15-d3_1_screen* qa/fastq_screen;
samtools index STAR/UNC-CR-R15-d3/UNC-CR-R15-d3Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam;
umi_tools dedup -I STAR/UNC-CR-R15-d3/UNC-CR-R15-d3Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam --output-stats=log/dedup/UNC-CR-R15-d3 -S umitools/UNC-CR-R15-d3-deduplicated.bam > log/UNC-CR-R15-d3_dedup.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes umitools/UNC-CR-R15-d3-deduplicated.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count_umi/UNC-CR-R15-d3_union_name.count;
umi_tools extract --stdin=raw/UNC-CR-R15-d5_1.fastq.gz --bc-pattern="^(?P<umi_1>.{6})(?P<discard_1>TATA){e<=1}" --extract-method=regex --log=log/UNC-CR-R15-d5_umi-tools.log --stdout umitools/umi_UNC-CR-R15-d5_1.fastq.gz;
fastqc -o qa/umitools umitools/umi_UNC-CR-R15-d5_1.fastq.gz;
TrimmomaticSE -threads 10 -phred33 umitools/umi_UNC-CR-R15-d5_1.fastq.gz trimmomatic/TRIM_UNC-CR-R15-d5_1.fastq HEADCROP:12 ILLUMINACLIP:/mnt/d/Adapters/Lexogen_quantseq.fa:2:30:10 LEADING:3 TRAILING:3 SLIDINGWINDOW:4:15 MINLEN:36 2> log/UNC-CR-R15-d5_trim.log;
fastqc -o qa/trimmomatic trimmomatic/TRIM_UNC-CR-R15-d5_1.fastq;
time sortmerna --ref /mnt/d/rRNA_database/mtDNA_homo_sapiens.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/mtDNA_homo_sapiens:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5.8s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5.8s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-16s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-16s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-16s-id90.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-16s-id90:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-18s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-18s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-28s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-28s-id98 --reads trimmomatic/TRIM_UNC-CR-R15-d5_1.fastq --aligned UNC-CR-R15-d5_aligned --other UNC-CR-R15-d5_sortmerna --log -a 10 -v --fastx;
mv UNC-CR-R15-d5_sortmerna.fastq sortmerna/sort_UNC-CR-R15-d5_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 trimmomatic/TRIM_UNC-CR-R15-d5_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 UNC-CR-R15-d5_aligned.fastq;
mv UNC-CR-R15-d5_aligned.fastq.gz sortmerna/;
mv UNC-CR-R15-d5_aligned.log log/;
fastqc -o qa/sortmerna sortmerna/sort_UNC-CR-R15-d5_1.fastq;

~/STAR-2.7.0f/bin/Linux_x86_64/STAR --genomeDir /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/ --readFilesIn sortmerna/sort_UNC-CR-R16-d7_1.fastq --runThreadN 10 --outFileNamePrefix STAR/UNC-CR-R16-d7/UNC-CR-R16-d7 --outFilterMultimapNmax 1 --outSAMtype BAM SortedByCoordinate;
pigz -p 12 sortmerna/sort_UNC-CR-R16-d7_1.fastq;
cp STAR/UNC-CR-R16-d7/UNC-CR-R16-d7Log.final.out log/UNC-CR-R16-d7_STAR.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes STAR/UNC-CR-R16-d7/UNC-CR-R16-d7Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count/UNC-CR-R16-d7_union_name.count;
~/fastq_screen_v0.11.1/fastq_screen --aligner bwa --threads 10 --conf /mnt/f/Genomes/fastq_screen/fastq_screen.conf sortmerna/sort_UNC-CR-R16-d7_1.fastq.gz;
mv sort_UNC-CR-R16-d7_1_screen* qa/fastq_screen;
samtools index STAR/UNC-CR-R16-d7/UNC-CR-R16-d7Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam;
umi_tools dedup -I STAR/UNC-CR-R16-d7/UNC-CR-R16-d7Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam --output-stats=log/dedup/UNC-CR-R16-d7 -S umitools/UNC-CR-R16-d7-deduplicated.bam > log/UNC-CR-R16-d7_dedup.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes umitools/UNC-CR-R16-d7-deduplicated.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count_umi/UNC-CR-R16-d7_union_name.count;
umi_tools extract --stdin=raw/UNC-CR-R16-d9_1.fastq.gz --bc-pattern="^(?P<umi_1>.{6})(?P<discard_1>TATA){e<=1}" --extract-method=regex --log=log/UNC-CR-R16-d9_umi-tools.log --stdout umitools/umi_UNC-CR-R16-d9_1.fastq.gz;
fastqc -o qa/umitools umitools/umi_UNC-CR-R16-d9_1.fastq.gz;
TrimmomaticSE -threads 10 -phred33 umitools/umi_UNC-CR-R16-d9_1.fastq.gz trimmomatic/TRIM_UNC-CR-R16-d9_1.fastq HEADCROP:12 ILLUMINACLIP:/mnt/d/Adapters/Lexogen_quantseq.fa:2:30:10 LEADING:3 TRAILING:3 SLIDINGWINDOW:4:15 MINLEN:36 2> log/UNC-CR-R16-d9_trim.log;

pigz -p 12 sortmerna/sort_UNC-R17-d9_1.fastq;

time sortmerna --ref /mnt/d/rRNA_database/mtDNA_homo_sapiens.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/mtDNA_homo_sapiens:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5.8s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5.8s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-16s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-16s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-16s-id90.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-16s-id90:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-18s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-18s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-28s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-28s-id98 --reads trimmomatic/TRIM_210715-C1_1.fastq --aligned 210715-C1_aligned --other 210715-C1_sortmerna --log -a 10 -v --fastx;
mv 210715-C1_sortmerna.fastq sortmerna/sort_210715-C1_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 trimmomatic/TRIM_210715-C1_1.fastq;

mv 210715-C1_aligned.fastq.gz sortmerna/;
mv 210715-C1_aligned.log log/;

mkdir STAR/210715-C1;
~/STAR-2.7.0f/bin/Linux_x86_64/STAR --genomeDir /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/ --readFilesIn sortmerna/sort_210715-C1_1.fastq --runThreadN 10 --outFileNamePrefix STAR/210715-C1/210715-C1 --outFilterMultimapNmax 1 --outSAMtype BAM SortedByCoordinate;
pigz -p 12 sortmerna/sort_210715-C1_1.fastq;

time sortmerna --ref /mnt/d/rRNA_database/mtDNA_homo_sapiens.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/mtDNA_homo_sapiens:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5.8s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5.8s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-16s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-16s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-16s-id90.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-16s-id90:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-18s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-18s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-28s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-28s-id98 --reads trimmomatic/TRIM_210722-G4_1.fastq --aligned 210722-G4_aligned --other 210722-G4_sortmerna --log -a 10 -v --fastx;
mv 210722-G4_sortmerna.fastq sortmerna/sort_210722-G4_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 trimmomatic/TRIM_210722-G4_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 210722-G4_aligned.fastq;
mv 210722-G4_aligned.fastq.gz sortmerna/;
mv 210722-G4_aligned.log log/;
fastqc -o qa/sortmerna sortmerna/sort_210722-G4_1.fastq;
mkdir STAR/210722-G4;
~/STAR-2.7.0f/bin/Linux_x86_64/STAR --genomeDir /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/ --readFilesIn sortmerna/sort_210722-G4_1.fastq --runThreadN 10 --outFileNamePrefix STAR/210722-G4/210722-G4 --outFilterMultimapNmax 1 --outSAMtype BAM SortedByCoordinate;
pigz -p 12 sortmerna/sort_210722-G4_1.fastq;
cp STAR/210722-G4/210722-G4Log.final.out log/210722-G4_STAR.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes STAR/210722-G4/210722-G4Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count/210722-G4_union_name.count;
~/fastq_screen_v0.11.1/fastq_screen --aligner bwa --threads 10 --conf /mnt/f/Genomes/fastq_screen/fastq_screen.conf sortmerna/sort_210722-G4_1.fastq.gz;
mv sort_210722-G4_1_screen* qa/fastq_screen;
samtools index STAR/210722-G4/210722-G4Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam;
umi_tools dedup -I STAR/210722-G4/210722-G4Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam --output-stats=log/dedup/210722-G4 -S umitools/210722-G4-deduplicated.bam > log/210722-G4_dedup.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes umitools/210722-G4-deduplicated.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count_umi/210722-G4_union_name.count;
umi_tools extract --stdin=raw/210722-V6_1.fastq.gz --bc-pattern="^(?P<umi_1>.{6})(?P<discard_1>TATA){e<=1}" --extract-method=regex --log=log/210722-V6_umi-tools.log --stdout umitools/umi_210722-V6_1.fastq.gz;
fastqc -o qa/umitools umitools/umi_210722-V6_1.fastq.gz;
TrimmomaticSE -threads 10 -phred33 umitools/umi_210722-V6_1.fastq.gz trimmomatic/TRIM_210722-V6_1.fastq HEADCROP:12 ILLUMINACLIP:/mnt/d/Adapters/Lexogen_quantseq.fa:2:30:10 LEADING:3 TRAILING:3 SLIDINGWINDOW:4:15 MINLEN:36 2> log/210722-V6_trim.log;
fastqc -o qa/trimmomatic trimmomatic/TRIM_210722-V6_1.fastq;
time sortmerna --ref /mnt/d/rRNA_database/mtDNA_homo_sapiens.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/mtDNA_homo_sapiens:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5.8s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5.8s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/rfam-5s-database-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/rfam-5s-database-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-16s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-16s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-arc-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-arc-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-16s-id90.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-16s-id90:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-bac-23s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-bac-23s-id98:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-18s-id95.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-18s-id95:/mnt/d/rRNA_database/silva-euk-28s-id98.fasta,/mnt/d/rRNA_database/index/silva-euk-28s-id98 --reads trimmomatic/TRIM_210722-V6_1.fastq --aligned 210722-V6_aligned --other 210722-V6_sortmerna --log -a 10 -v --fastx;
mv 210722-V6_sortmerna.fastq sortmerna/sort_210722-V6_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 trimmomatic/TRIM_210722-V6_1.fastq;
pigz -p 12 210722-V6_aligned.fastq;
mv 210722-V6_aligned.fastq.gz sortmerna/;
mv 210722-V6_aligned.log log/;
fastqc -o qa/sortmerna sortmerna/sort_210722-V6_1.fastq;
mkdir STAR/210722-V6;
~/STAR-2.7.0f/bin/Linux_x86_64/STAR --genomeDir /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/ --readFilesIn sortmerna/sort_210722-V6_1.fastq --runThreadN 10 --outFileNamePrefix STAR/210722-V6/210722-V6 --outFilterMultimapNmax 1 --outSAMtype BAM SortedByCoordinate;
pigz -p 12 sortmerna/sort_210722-V6_1.fastq;
cp STAR/210722-V6/210722-V6Log.final.out log/210722-V6_STAR.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes STAR/210722-V6/210722-V6Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count/210722-V6_union_name.count;
~/fastq_screen_v0.11.1/fastq_screen --aligner bwa --threads 10 --conf /mnt/f/Genomes/fastq_screen/fastq_screen.conf sortmerna/sort_210722-V6_1.fastq.gz;
mv sort_210722-V6_1_screen* qa/fastq_screen;
samtools index STAR/210722-V6/210722-V6Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam;
umi_tools dedup -I STAR/210722-V6/210722-V6Aligned.sortedByCoord.out.bam --output-stats=log/dedup/210722-V6 -S umitools/210722-V6-deduplicated.bam > log/210722-V6_dedup.log;
htseq-count -f bam -i gene_id -r pos -m union -s yes umitools/210722-V6-deduplicated.bam /mnt/f/Genomes/Homo_sapiens_GRCh38/Homo_sapiens.GRCh38.87.gtf > count_umi/210722-V6_union_name.count;
